<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понижение.html>пониже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponižénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понижение.html>пониже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понижение.html>пониже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понижение.html>пониже́ний</a></b>)

<ol><li>fall, lowering, drop, reduction

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:понижение.html>пониже́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:давление.html>давле́ния</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ponižénije</b> davlénija</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">pressure drop</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:понижение.html>пониже́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уровень.html>у́ровня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ponižénije</b> úrovnja vody</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">sinking/abatement of the water level</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:понижение.html>пониже́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жбе</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ponižénije</b> po slúžbe</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">demotion</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:понижение.html>пониже́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заработный.html>за́работной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плат.html>пла́ты</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ponižénije</b> zárabotnoj pláty</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">wage cut</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понижение.html>пониже́ние</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">igrátʹ na <b>ponižénije</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">speculate for a fall; sell short; bear</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

***понизивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зивший</a> (8438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зивший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponízivšij</span>)
</p>

***понизить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зить</a> (8438)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:низ.html>ни́з</a>(<a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a>)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">níz(kij)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a factitive construction.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponízitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понижать.html>понижа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lower, to reduce
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ponízitʹ</b> cény</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lower/reduce prices</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ponízitʹ</b> gólos</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lower/drop one's voice</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to demote
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пониженный.html>пони́жен</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звание.html>зва́нии</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on byl <b>ponížen</b> v zvánii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he was demoted/lowered in rank</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снизить.html>сни́зить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">snízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уменьшить.html>уме́ньшить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uménʹšitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понизиться.html>пони́зиться</a> (30348)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ponízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понизиться.html>пони́зиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponízitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понижаться.html>понижа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to decrease, to go down, to drop <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of temperature, prices, a rate, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понизить.html>пони́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ponízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зить<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:понижаться.html>понижа́ться</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ть</a> (140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понять.html>поня́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to understand, to comprehend, to see
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ю</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́те</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne <b>ponimáju</b>, što vy govoríte.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't understand what you're saying.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to realize, to appreciate</li></ol>

***понимающе.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимающий.html>понимающе</a> (9798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ющий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ponimájuščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-e</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимающий.html>понима́юще</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponimájušče</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>knowingly, consciously</li>
<li>intelligently</li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понос.html>поно́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponós</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понос.html>поно́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понос.html>поно́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понос.html>поно́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>diarrhea</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> too much of something that is incapable to stop itself

***поносить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поносить.html>поно́сить</a> (14740)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поносить.html>поноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to carry something (for a while)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear clothes, to shoes (for a while)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потаскать.html>потаска́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potaskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unclear. Difficult to derive from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is almost always a perfectivizing prefix.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поносить.html>поноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to vilify, to criticize, to insult</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***понравиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понравиться.html>понра́виться</a> (1217)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́виться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nrávitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понравиться.html>понра́виться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponrávitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́виться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to like (<i>the person who likes is the object of the verb, in dative</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кино.html>кино́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понравиться.html>понра́вилось</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto kinó mne ne <b>ponrávilosʹ</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I didn't like this movie.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to please</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>понт</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> ??  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-понт-</b>.

<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="региональное">рег.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;"><a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>обы́чно</a> <i><span title="множественное число" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">мн. ч.</span></i></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рог</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:северный.html>се́верного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:олень.html>оле́ня</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:обыватель.html>Обыва́тели</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>веду́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сонный.html>со́нную</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пьяный.html>пья́ную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вообще.html>вообще́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живу́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:впроголодь.html>впро́голодь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:послать.html>посла́л</a>. Пробавляются <a href = vnd.unilang:поставка.html>поста́вками</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> Сахалин, <a href = vnd.unilang:золотой.html>золоты́м</a> хищничеством, <a href = vnd.unilang:эксплуатация.html>эксплуата́цией</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:инородец.html>иноро́дцев</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:продажа.html>прода́жей</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:понт.html>понтов</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:олений.html>оле́ньих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рого́в</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:китаец.html>кита́йцы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приготовлять.html>приготовля́ют</a> возбудительные <a href = vnd.unilang:пилюля.html>пилю́ли</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2,_%D0%90%D0%BD%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BD_%D0%9F%D0%B0%D0%B2%D0%BB%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Чехов, Антон Павлович"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. П. <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a></a>, «<a href="https://ru.wikisource.org/wiki/%D0%9E%D1%81%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2_%D0%A1%D0%B0%D1%85%D0%B0%D0%BB%D0%B8%D0%BD_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:Остров Сахалин (Чехов)"><a href = vnd.unilang:остров.html>О́стров</a> Сахалин</a>», <span class="example-date">1893–1895 гг.<span class="citation-source"> <span class="nkrja-source" style="font-size: x-small; font-style: italic;"></span></span></span></i></span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понятливый.html>поня́тливый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponjátlivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>apt, quick-witted <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">mentally keen</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня́т<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>поня́тливее, поня́тливей.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-поня-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-т-лив</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***понятно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понятно.html>поня́тно</a> (976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понятный.html>поня́тный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ponjátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понятно.html>поня́тно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponjátno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>understandably, comprehensibly</li>
<li>clearly, plainly</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конечно.html>коне́чно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">konečno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:естественно.html>есте́ственно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jestéstvenno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разуметься.html>разуме́ется</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razuméjetsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понятый.html>понятой</a> (14595)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понятый.html>понято́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponjatój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понятый.html>понято́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понятый.html>поняты́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понятый.html>поняты́х</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понятый.html>понята́я</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:понять.html>поня́ть</a> (125)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понять.html>поня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ponjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to understand, to comprehend, to see
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:понять.html>по́нял</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">radio</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Pónjal</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">roger, copy, understood</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to realize, to appreciate</li></ol>
